features\staff\data\worker_model.dart[
    import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';

class WorkerModel {
  final String? id;
  final String name;
  final String role;
  final double salary;
  final String mobile;
  final DateTime joinDate;
  final bool isActive;

  WorkerModel({
    this.id,
    required this.name,
    required this.role,
    required this.salary,
    required this.mobile,
    required this.joinDate,
    this.isActive = true,
  });

  Map<String, dynamic> toMap() {
    return {
      'name': name,
      'role': role,
      'salary': salary,
      'mobile': mobile,
      'joinDate': Timestamp.fromDate(joinDate),
      'isActive': isActive,
    };
  }

  factory WorkerModel.fromSnapshot(DocumentSnapshot snap) {
    final data = snap.data() as Map<String, dynamic>;
    return WorkerModel(
      id: snap.id,
      name: data['name'] ?? '',
      role: data['role'] ?? '',
      salary: (data['salary'] ?? 0).toDouble(),
      mobile: data['mobile'] ?? '',
      joinDate: (data['joinDate'] as Timestamp).toDate(),
      isActive: data['isActive'] ?? true,
    );
  }
}

]
features\staff\presentation\add_worker_screen.dart[
    import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import '../../../core/services/firestore_service.dart';
import '../../auth/presentation/widgets/auth_widgets.dart'; // For ClayTextField and Button
import '../data/worker_model.dart';

class AddWorkerScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final WorkerModel? worker; // If not null, we are in Edit mode

  const AddWorkerScreen({super.key, this.worker});

  @override
  State<AddWorkerScreen> createState() => _AddWorkerScreenState();
}

class _AddWorkerScreenState extends State<AddWorkerScreen> {
  final _nameController = TextEditingController();
  final _roleController = TextEditingController();
  final _salaryController = TextEditingController();
  final _mobileController = TextEditingController();
  final FirestoreService _service = FirestoreService();
  bool _isLoading = false;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();
    if (widget.worker != null) {
      _nameController.text = widget.worker!.name;
      _roleController.text = widget.worker!.role;
      _salaryController.text = widget.worker!.salary.toString();
      _mobileController.text = widget.worker!.mobile;
    }
  }

  Future<void> _saveWorker() async {
    if (_nameController.text.isEmpty || _salaryController.text.isEmpty) {
      showTopToast(context, "Name and Salary are required", isError: true);
      return;
    }

    setState(() => _isLoading = true);

    try {
      final workerData = {
        'name': _nameController.text.trim(),
        'role': _roleController.text.trim(),
        'salary': double.tryParse(_salaryController.text) ?? 0.0,
        'mobile': _mobileController.text.trim(),
        'joinDate': widget.worker?.joinDate ?? DateTime.now(),
        'isActive': widget.worker?.isActive ?? true,
        'updatedAt': DateTime.now(),
      };

      if (widget.worker != null) {
        await _service.updateWorker(widget.worker!.id!, workerData);
      } else {
        await _service.addWorker(workerData);
      }

      if (mounted) Navigator.pop(context);
    } catch (e) {
      if (mounted) {
        showTopToast(context, "Error: ${e.toString()}", isError: true);
      }
    } finally {
      if (mounted) setState(() => _isLoading = false);
    }
  }

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: Text(widget.worker == null ? "Add Worker" : "Edit Worker"),
        backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
        elevation: 0,
        iconTheme: const IconThemeData(color: Colors.black87),
      ),
      body: SingleChildScrollView(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(25),
        child: Column(
          children: [
            ClayTextField(
              controller: _nameController,
              hint: "Full Name",
              icon: Icons.person,
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 20),
            ClayTextField(
              controller: _roleController,
              hint: "Role (e.g. Sales, Helper)",
              icon: Icons.work,
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 20),
            ClayTextField(
              controller: _salaryController,
              hint: "Monthly Salary (₹)",
              icon: Icons.currency_rupee,
              keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 20),
            ClayTextField(
              controller: _mobileController,
              hint: "Mobile Number",
              icon: Icons.phone,
              keyboardType: TextInputType.phone,
            ),
            const SizedBox(height: 40),
            _isLoading
                ? const CircularProgressIndicator()
                : ClayPrimaryButton(
                    text: widget.worker == null
                        ? "ADD WORKER"
                        : "UPDATE WORKER",
                    onTap: _saveWorker,
                  ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

features\staff\presentation\workers_screen.dart[
    import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:clay_containers/clay_containers.dart';
import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
import '../../../core/localization/app_strings.dart';
import '../../../core/services/firestore_service.dart';
import '../data/worker_model.dart';
import 'add_worker_screen.dart';
import 'worker_detail_screen.dart';

class WorkersScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  const WorkersScreen({super.key});

  @override
  State<WorkersScreen> createState() => _WorkersScreenState();
}

class _WorkersScreenState extends State<WorkersScreen> {
  final FirestoreService _service = FirestoreService();

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: Text(
          AppStrings.get('workerList'),
          style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.black87),
        ),
        backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
        elevation: 0,
        iconTheme: const IconThemeData(color: Colors.black87),
      ),
      floatingActionButton: FloatingActionButton(
        onPressed: () => Navigator.push(
          context,
          MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const AddWorkerScreen()),
        ),
        backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFFF9800),
        child: const Icon(Icons.add),
      ),
      body: StreamBuilder<QuerySnapshot>(
        stream: _service.getWorkersStream(),
        builder: (context, snapshot) {
          if (snapshot.connectionState == ConnectionState.waiting) {
            return const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator());
          }

          if (!snapshot.hasData || snapshot.data!.docs.isEmpty) {
            return Center(
              child: Column(
                mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
                children: [
                  Icon(
                    Icons.engineering_outlined,
                    size: 80,
                    color: Colors.grey[300],
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 16),
                  const Text(
                    "No workers added yet",
                    style: TextStyle(color: Colors.grey),
                  ),
                ],
              ),
            );
          }

          return ListView.builder(
            padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
            itemCount: snapshot.data!.docs.length,
            itemBuilder: (context, index) {
              final worker = WorkerModel.fromSnapshot(
                snapshot.data!.docs[index],
              );
              return _buildWorkerCard(worker);
            },
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildWorkerCard(WorkerModel worker) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 20.0),
      child: InkWell(
        onTap: () {
          Navigator.push(
            context,
            MaterialPageRoute(
              builder: (_) => WorkerDetailScreen(worker: worker),
            ),
          );
        },
        child: ClayContainer(
          color: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
          borderRadius: 20,
          depth: 15,
          child: Padding(
            padding: const EdgeInsets.all(15.0),
            child: Row(
              children: [
                CircleAvatar(
                  radius: 30,
                  backgroundColor: Colors.blue[50],
                  child: const Icon(Icons.person, color: Colors.blue, size: 30),
                ),
                const SizedBox(width: 15),
                Expanded(
                  child: Column(
                    crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                    children: [
                      Text(
                        worker.name,
                        style: const TextStyle(
                          fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                          fontSize: 16,
                        ),
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(height: 5),
                      Text(
                        "${worker.role} • ${worker.mobile}",
                        style: const TextStyle(
                          color: Colors.grey,
                          fontSize: 12,
                        ),
                      ),
                      const SizedBox(height: 8),
                      // Today's Attendance Status
                      StreamBuilder<QuerySnapshot>(
                        stream: _service.getAttendanceForDateStream(
                          worker.id!,
                          DateTime.now(),
                        ),
                        builder: (context, attSnapshot) {
                          bool isPresent = false;
                          if (attSnapshot.hasData &&
                              attSnapshot.data!.docs.isNotEmpty) {
                            isPresent =
                                (attSnapshot.data!.docs.first.data()
                                    as Map)['isPresent'] ??
                                false;
                          }

                          return Row(
                            children: [
                              Icon(
                                isPresent
                                    ? Icons.check_circle
                                    : Icons.radio_button_unchecked,
                                size: 14,
                                color: isPresent ? Colors.green : Colors.grey,
                              ),
                              const SizedBox(width: 5),
                              Text(
                                isPresent
                                    ? AppStrings.get('present')
                                    : "Mark Today",
                                style: TextStyle(
                                  color: isPresent ? Colors.green : Colors.grey,
                                  fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                                  fontSize: 12,
                                ),
                              ),
                              if (!isPresent)
                                IconButton(
                                  icon: const Icon(
                                    Icons.check,
                                    size: 16,
                                    color: Colors.green,
                                  ),
                                  onPressed: () => _service.markAttendance(
                                    worker.id!,
                                    DateTime.now(),
                                    true,
                                  ),
                                  padding: EdgeInsets.zero,
                                  constraints: const BoxConstraints(),
                                ),
                            ],
                          );
                        },
                      ),
                    ],
                  ),
                ),
                Column(
                  children: [
                    const Text(
                      "Salary Due",
                      style: TextStyle(fontSize: 10, color: Colors.grey),
                    ),
                    Text(
                      "₹${worker.salary.toStringAsFixed(0)}",
                      style: const TextStyle(
                        fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                        color: Colors.red,
                        fontSize: 16,
                      ),
                    ),
                    const SizedBox(height: 5),
                    GestureDetector(
                      onTap: () {
                        // Note: Implementation pending for Advance/Pay
                      },
                      child: ClayContainer(
                        height: 30,
                        width: 70,
                        borderRadius: 15,
                        depth: 5,
                        color: const Color(0xFFE8F5E9),
                        child: const Center(
                          child: Text(
                            "PAY",
                            style: TextStyle(
                              fontSize: 12,
                              fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                              color: Colors.green,
                            ),
                          ),
                        ),
                      ),
                    ),
                  ],
                ),
              ],
            ),
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }
}

features\staff\presentation\worker_detail_screen.dart[
    import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
import 'package:clay_containers/clay_containers.dart';
import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
import 'package:intl/intl.dart';
import '../../../core/services/firestore_service.dart';
import '../../auth/presentation/widgets/auth_widgets.dart';
import '../data/worker_model.dart';
import 'add_worker_screen.dart';

class WorkerDetailScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  final WorkerModel worker;

  const WorkerDetailScreen({super.key, required this.worker});

  @override
  State<WorkerDetailScreen> createState() => _WorkerDetailScreenState();
}

class _WorkerDetailScreenState extends State<WorkerDetailScreen> {
  final FirestoreService _service = FirestoreService();

  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Scaffold(
      backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
      appBar: AppBar(
        title: Text(widget.worker.name),
        backgroundColor: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
        elevation: 0,
        iconTheme: const IconThemeData(color: Colors.black87),
        actions: [
          IconButton(
            icon: const Icon(Icons.edit),
            onPressed: () => Navigator.push(
              context,
              MaterialPageRoute(
                builder: (_) => AddWorkerScreen(worker: widget.worker),
              ),
            ),
          ),
        ],
      ),
      body: SingleChildScrollView(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20),
        child: Column(
          crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
          children: [
            _buildHeader(),
            const SizedBox(height: 30),
            _buildActionButtons(),
            const SizedBox(height: 30),
            _buildSectionTitle("Recent Attendance"),
            _buildAttendanceList(),
            const SizedBox(height: 30),
            _buildSectionTitle("Recent Advances"),
            _buildAdvancesList(),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildHeader() {
    return ClayContainer(
      color: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
      borderRadius: 20,
      depth: 15,
      child: Padding(
        padding: const EdgeInsets.all(20.0),
        child: Row(
          children: [
            CircleAvatar(
              radius: 40,
              backgroundColor: Colors.blue[50],
              child: const Icon(Icons.person, color: Colors.blue, size: 40),
            ),
            const SizedBox(width: 20),
            Expanded(
              child: Column(
                crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
                children: [
                  Text(
                    widget.worker.name,
                    style: const TextStyle(
                      fontSize: 20,
                      fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                    ),
                  ),
                  Text(
                    widget.worker.role,
                    style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.grey),
                  ),
                  const SizedBox(height: 10),
                  Text("Mobile: ${widget.worker.mobile}"),
                  Text(
                    "Salary: ₹${widget.worker.salary.toStringAsFixed(0)} / month",
                  ),
                ],
              ),
            ),
          ],
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildActionButtons() {
    return Row(
      children: [
        Expanded(
          child: _buildActionButton(
            "Mark Present",
            Icons.check_circle,
            Colors.green,
            () => _service.markAttendance(
              widget.worker.id!,
              DateTime.now(),
              true,
            ),
          ),
        ),
        const SizedBox(width: 15),
        Expanded(
          child: _buildActionButton(
            "Add Advance",
            Icons.money_off,
            Colors.orange,
            _showAdvanceDialog,
          ),
        ),
      ],
    );
  }

  Widget _buildActionButton(
    String label,
    IconData icon,
    Color color,
    VoidCallback onTap,
  ) {
    return GestureDetector(
      onTap: onTap,
      child: ClayContainer(
        color: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
        borderRadius: 15,
        depth: 10,
        child: Padding(
          padding: const EdgeInsets.all(15.0),
          child: Column(
            children: [
              Icon(icon, color: color),
              const SizedBox(height: 5),
              Text(
                label,
                style: TextStyle(
                  color: color,
                  fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
                  fontSize: 12,
                ),
              ),
            ],
          ),
        ),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildSectionTitle(String title) {
    return Padding(
      padding: const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: 15.0),
      child: Text(
        title,
        style: const TextStyle(fontSize: 18, fontWeight: FontWeight.bold),
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildAttendanceList() {
    // For simplicity, we'll just show the last few days
    return ClayContainer(
      color: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
      borderRadius: 15,
      depth: 10,
      child: StreamBuilder<QuerySnapshot>(
        stream: _service.getRecentAttendanceStream(widget.worker.id!, limit: 5),
        builder: (context, snapshot) {
          if (!snapshot.hasData || snapshot.data!.docs.isEmpty) {
            return const Padding(
              padding: EdgeInsets.all(16.0),
              child: Center(child: Text("No attendance records found")),
            );
          }
          return ListView.separated(
            shrinkWrap: true,
            physics: const NeverScrollableScrollPhysics(),
            itemCount: snapshot.data!.docs.length,
            separatorBuilder: (context, index) => const Divider(height: 1),
            itemBuilder: (context, index) {
              final data =
                  snapshot.data!.docs[index].data() as Map<String, dynamic>;
              final date = (data['date'] as Timestamp).toDate();
              final isPresent = data['isPresent'] as bool;
              return ListTile(
                leading: Icon(
                  isPresent ? Icons.check_circle : Icons.cancel,
                  color: isPresent ? Colors.green : Colors.red,
                ),
                title: Text(DateFormat('EEEE, MMM d').format(date)),
                trailing: Text(
                  isPresent ? "Present" : "Absent",
                  style: TextStyle(
                    color: isPresent ? Colors.green : Colors.red,
                  ),
                ),
              );
            },
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }

  Widget _buildAdvancesList() {
    return ClayContainer(
      color: const Color(0xFFF2F4F8),
      borderRadius: 15,
      depth: 10,
      child: StreamBuilder<QuerySnapshot>(
        stream: _service.getRecentAdvancesStream(widget.worker.id!, limit: 5),
        builder: (context, snapshot) {
          if (!snapshot.hasData || snapshot.data!.docs.isEmpty) {
            return const Padding(
              padding: EdgeInsets.all(16.0),
              child: Center(child: Text("No advances recorded")),
            );
          }
          return ListView.separated(
            shrinkWrap: true,
            physics: const NeverScrollableScrollPhysics(),
            itemCount: snapshot.data!.docs.length,
            separatorBuilder: (context, index) => const Divider(height: 1),
            itemBuilder: (context, index) {
              final data =
                  snapshot.data!.docs[index].data() as Map<String, dynamic>;
              final date = (data['date'] as Timestamp).toDate();
              final amount = data['amount'] as double;
              return ListTile(
                leading: const Icon(Icons.arrow_upward, color: Colors.orange),
                title: Text("Advance: ₹${amount.toStringAsFixed(0)}"),
                subtitle: Text(DateFormat('MMM d, yyyy').format(date)),
              );
            },
          );
        },
      ),
    );
  }

  void _showAdvanceDialog() {
    final amountController = TextEditingController();
    final reasonController = TextEditingController();
    showDialog(
      context: context,
      builder: (context) => AlertDialog(
        title: const Text("Add Advance"),
        content: Column(
          mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
          children: [
            TextField(
              controller: amountController,
              decoration: const InputDecoration(labelText: "Amount (₹)"),
              keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
            ),
            TextField(
              controller: reasonController,
              decoration: const InputDecoration(labelText: "Reason (Optional)"),
            ),
          ],
        ),
        actions: [
          TextButton(
            onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
            child: const Text("Cancel"),
          ),
          ElevatedButton(
            onPressed: () {
              final amount = double.tryParse(amountController.text) ?? 0.0;
              if (amount > 0) {
                _service.addAdvance(
                  widget.worker.id!,
                  amount,
                  reasonController.text,
                );
                Navigator.pop(context);
                showTopToast(context, "Advance added successfully");
              }
            },
            child: const Text("Add"),
          ),
        ],
      ),
    );
  }
}

]
